<description>
<![CDATA[ <strong>Civil Designer</strong><br> Locations: Salt Lake City, UT or Kansas City, MO (Hybrid) <br> <br> Benefits: Access to Client Benefits Package <br> <br> <u><strong>Responsibilities: </strong></u> <ul> <li>Designers are expected to observe professional ethics in their association with others including fellow employees, clients, and vendors</li> <li>Reviews rough sketches, drawings, specifications, and other engineering data received from the Engineer.</li> <li>Reviews project scope of work and notify project management of any perceived changes in scope that may appear during the design phase.</li> <li>Reviews the design input and communicates any ambiguous, incomplete, or conflicting information to the supplier of the input for resolution (includes processing information such as vendor drawings, marked up drawings, design basis, notes, and verbal instructions).</li> <li>Reviews design output to verify it meets design input (i.e., verify output meets design basis, design input and standard industry practices).</li> <li>Track and log all design decisions.</li> <li>Performs work related to design changes after validated documents are issued and notify project management of any perceived changes in scope resulting from the change.</li> </ul> <br> <u><strong>Requirements: </strong></u> <ul> <li>A high level of competency in AutoCAD Civil 3D is required.</li> <li>An associate degree (A. A.) or equivalent from two-year college or technical school; and 5 to 7+ years’ experience and/or training; or equivalent combination of education and experience.</li> <li>Ability to review survey data from multiple sources, utilizing Civil 3D Grading, Corridor and Rail design tools.</li> <li>Ability to coordinate scope hand-offs between other disciplines.</li> <li>Communicate Civil 3D design and scope through Navisworks for all underground piping, roadway/rail designs, and 3D grading models.</li> <li>Ability to communicate effectively with all levels of professionals and all aspects of the industrial design process including but not limited to, process engineers, electrical and instrumentation engineers, architects etc.</li> </ul> <br> <em>We are an Equal Opportunity Employer and do not discriminate on the basis of race, color, religion, sex, national origin, age, disability, veteran status, genetic information, sexual orientation, gender identity, or any other legally protected status. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to any of these characteristics.</em><br> ]]>

<![CDATA[ <p>You will be responsible for the development of integrated circuits operating at speeds greater than 100Gbaud for next-generation products. This role involves driving multiple aspects of IC product development, including circuit design, physical layout, and silicon bring-up. You will collaborate closely with teams across verification, CAD, product engineering, and test engineering to create and execute detailed design validation test (DVT) plans and device characterization strategies.</p> <hr> <p><strong>KEY SKILLS AND EXPERIENCE</strong></p> <p><strong>Minimum Experience Requirements:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>Proven experience in high-speed analog IC design using SiGe BiCMOS or CMOS technologies</p> <li> <p>Strong understanding of transmission lines and other high-frequency passive components</p> <li> <p>Solid grasp of device physics and its influence on analog circuit performance, along with techniques to optimize performance</p> <li> <p>Hands-on experience with RF wafer probing, lab instrumentation, and evaluation of high-speed analog ICs</p> <li> <p>Familiarity with Verilog-A and scripting languages such as Skill, Python, or shell scripts is an asset</p> <li> <p>Excellent teamwork, verbal, and written communication skills</p> </ul> <p><strong>Education Requirements:</strong></p> <ul> <li> <p>BS with 5+ years of relevant experience</p> <li> <p>MS with 3+ years of relevant experience</p> <li> <p>PhD with related academic or professional experience</p> </ul> ]]>

<![CDATA[ <p>We are seeking a highly skilled <strong>Technical Architect</strong> to design and implement robust technology architectures, frameworks, and strategies that align with business objectives and application requirements. standards, and requirements that influence solution design.</p> <li> <p><strong>Solution Evaluation</strong>: Analyze and assess alternative technology solutions to determine the most effective approach to business challenges.</p> <li> <p><strong>Integration Leadership</strong>: Ensure seamless integration of all components within technology solutions.</p> <li> <p><strong>Trend Monitoring</strong>: Stay current with industry and government technology trends to align solutions with evolving directions.</p> <li> <p><strong>Innovation & Emerging Tech</strong>: Provide insight, direction, and support for the adoption of emerging technologies.</p> <li> <p><strong>Impact Analysis</strong>: Conduct impact assessments of proposed technology changes on systems and operations.</p> <li> <p><strong>Support & Guidance</strong>: Collaborate with application development and technical support teams to ensure optimal use of infrastructure.</p> <li> <p><strong>Standards & Performance</strong>: Review application and infrastructure designs for compliance with standards, recommending enhancements for performance and scalability.</p> <li> <p><strong>Executive tools (iPerf).</p> <li> <p>Validate networking features and performance across <strong>OSI layers</strong>, including TCP, UDP, IP networking, routing protocols, and network optimization techniques.</p> <li> <p>Implement and manage <strong>NETCONF</strong> and <strong>gRPC/gNMI</strong> for automated network device configuration.</p> <li> <p>Work with structured <strong>data threat modeling and security risk assessments for satellite hardware, software, and communication systems.</p> <li> <p><strong>Secure Design & Architecture:</strong> Collaborate with engineering teams to design secure systems, including onboard satellite software, ground control systems, and data links.</p> <li> <p><strong>Vulnerability Management:</strong> Evaluate and support remediation efforts related to vulnerabilities in embedded systems, firmware, and satellite communication protocols.</p> <li> <p><strong>Security Testing:</strong> Propose test use cases and review testing results for assessments such as penetration testing, fuzzing, and static/dynamic code analysis on satellite and ground systems.</p> <li> <p><strong>Compliance & Standards:</strong> Ensure compliance with industry standards/frameworks such as NIST, ISO 27001, and space-specific cybersecurity frameworks (e.g., CCSDS, CNSSI 1253).</p> <li> <p><strong>Incident Response:</strong> Create concepts of operation for incident detection, analysis, and response to security events affecting satellite products.</p> <li> <p><strong>Tooling & Automation:</strong> Ensure the software development lifecycle follows industry best practices and utilize appropriate security tools to automate security checks.</p> <li> <p><strong>Collaboration:</strong> Work cross-functionally with software, hardware, systems, and mission assurance teams to champion security best practices.</p> </ul> <h3>Education/Experience</h3> <ul> <li> <p>Bachelor’s or Master’s degree in Computer Science, Electrical Engineering, Cybersecurity, or a related field.</p> <li> <p>10+ years of experience in product or embedded security architecture.</p> <li> <p>Experience in the aerospace or satellite industry.</p> <li> <p>Certifications such as CISSP, OSCP, CEH, or GIAC.</p> </ul> <h3>Specialized Knowledge, Skills and Abilities</h3> <ul> <li> <p>Strong understanding of embedded systems security, real-time operating systems (RTOS), and secure communications.</p> <li> <p>Knowledge of space system architectures, including satellite buses, payloads, and ground stations.</p> <li> <p>Extensive understanding of the space industry threat landscape.</p> <li> <p>Experience with security tools (e.g., SAST, DAST, Splunk).</p> <li> <p>Knowledge of cybersecurity frameworks (e.g., NIST 800-53, ISO/IEC 27001).</p> <li> <p>Familiarity with space situational awareness (SSA) and anti-jamming/anti-spoofing techniques.</p> <li> <p>Experience with DevSecOps in aerospace environments.</p> </ul> ]]>

<![CDATA[ &lt;p&gt;Myticas's direct client is seeking &lt;strong&gt;Project Manager&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;for 12+&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Months Contract&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; role. Will need to be onsite from day 1, two days a week. Local candidates only - Candidates must be located within 2 hours of Lansing, MI at time of submission.&lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Top Skills &amp; Years of Experience:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; - 5+ years overall experience&lt;br&gt; - Experience with the &lt;strong&gt;ADKAR (Prosci) Framework&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; - Proven ability to &lt;strong&gt;lead large, cross-functional teams and manage high-visibility projects with medium to high risk.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; - Strong leadership, interpersonal, and communication skills with experience interacting with Agency Leadership.&lt;br&gt; - Ability to manage both technical delivery and change management efforts within complex environments.&lt;br&gt; - Demonstrated success managing vendor-supported projects with integrated technical components and stakeholder groups.&lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Job Summary:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; The State of Michigan is seeking an experienced and dynamic Senior Project Manager to lead complex, large-scale IT initiatives. This role requires a strong blend of project management expertise, leadership capabilities, technical awareness, and change management proficiency to ensure successful project outcomes aligned with business objectives and enterprise standards.&lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Key Responsibilities:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/h3&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Provide strategic oversight, leadership, and accountability for one or more large, complex IT projects, typically lasting longer than 6 months, involving 20 or more team members, and requiring executive-level communication and coordination. &lt;li&gt;Ensure alignment with State of Michigan project management methodologies, including SUITE, investment management, and systems engineering methodology. &lt;li&gt;Lead cross-functional teams through all phases of project planning and execution, including the development of integrated schedules, risk management plans, and budget tracking. &lt;li&gt;Monitor and report on project progress regarding scope, quality, schedule, and budget, and escalate issues and risks to executive leadership as necessary. &lt;li&gt;Perform long-term release planning to support organizational strategic goals and ensure alignment with broader enterprise initiatives. &lt;li&gt;Evaluate technical requirements in collaboration with IT and business stakeholders, proposing solutions that meet business needs while adhering to SOM best practices and industry standards. &lt;li&gt;Apply structured change management practices grounded in the ADKAR (Prosci) framework to ensure stakeholder alignment and successful adoption of project deliverables. &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Technical Competencies:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Strong knowledge of APIs, system interfaces, and multi-system integrations across complex IT environments. &lt;li&gt;Working knowledge of IT infrastructure components and their interactions within networked environments (e.g., firewalls, VIPs, F5 listeners, ports). &lt;li&gt;Familiarity with core infrastructure environments including networks, servers, storage, web platforms, and virtual/cloud solutions. &lt;li&gt;Ability to effectively collaborate with technical teams and external vendors to support solution design, integration, deployment, and issue resolution. &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Change Management and Stakeholder Engagement:&lt;/strong&gt; This position plays a critical role in driving change adoption through: &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Integration of change management principles from the outset of the project. &lt;li&gt;Close collaboration with stakeholder engagement leads to develop and implement communication plans, facilitate training sessions, and monitor organizational readiness. &lt;li&gt;Supporting stakeholders at every level to reduce resistance, align expectations, and ensure long-term user adoption of new systems and processes. &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Ideal Candidate Profile:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Proven ability to lead large, cross-functional teams and manage high-visibility projects with medium to high risk. &lt;li&gt;Strong leadership, interpersonal, and communication skills with experience interacting with Agency Leadership. &lt;li&gt;Ability to manage both technical delivery and change management efforts within complex environments. &lt;li&gt;Demonstrated success managing vendor-supported projects with integrated technical components and stakeholder groups. &lt;/ul&gt; <![CDATA[ &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Title: &lt;/strong&gt;Cyber Posture Management Analyst&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Type: &lt;/strong&gt;Direct Hire&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Location: &lt;/strong&gt;Lansing, Michigan&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Clover Consulting (a Myticas Co.) has a large, direct client seeking a skilled Cyber Posture Mgmt. Analyst I to join the team as part of their Information Security &amp; Privacy team. This role requires knowledge across multiple platforms, applications, processes, and procedures to enable access management of business initiatives across the enterprise.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;Essential Responsibilities&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Familiar with identity and access management, with a focus on Privileged Access Management (PAM), Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA), and Identity Governance and Administration (IGA). &lt;li&gt;Knowledge of scripting languages (e.g., PowerShell, Python) for automation and customization of IAM solutions. &lt;li&gt;Understanding of identity protocols and technologies: OpenID Connect (OIDC,) OAuth, SAML, AD-Fed, API Gateways, SCIM, and platforms such as, Sailpoint, CyberArk, and MS Entra. &lt;li&gt;Knowledge of identity &amp; They can also take on an increasing role of ownership on electrical and controls packages and management of project tasks.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;ESSENTIAL FUNCTIONS&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Designers are expected to observe professional ethics in their association with others including fellow employees, clients, and vendors&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Reviews rough sketches, drawings, specifications, and other engineering data received from the Engineer.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Reviews project scope of work and notify project management of any perceived changes in scope that may appear during the design phase.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Reviews the design input and communicates any ambiguous, incomplete, or conflicting information to the supplier of the input for resolution (includes processing information such as vendor drawings, marked up drawings, design basis, notes, and verbal instructions).&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Reviews design output to verify it meets design input (i.e., verify output meets design basis, design input and standard industry practices).&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Performs work related to design changes after validated documents are issued and notify project management of any perceived changes in scope resulting from the change.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Conform to drafting and quality standards&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Design electrical and control systems. Generate drawings in accordance with client design requirement for execution and productivity&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;-Draw single line diagrams (SLD), elementary diagrams (ED), power distribution diagrams, grounding diagrams, lighting drawing, logic diagrams, network architecture diagrams, function diagrams, and other drawings using AutoCAD and other CAD software.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;OTHER SKILLS AND ABILITIES&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;A high level of competency in AutoCAD is required. The ability to create, modify reference and plot drawings to client standards is key to this position. Knowledge of PDS EE Raceway, SmartPlant Electrical and/or SKM is a plus. Basic knowledge of applicable codes and standards such as NEC, ISA, NFPA, ANSI, OSHA etc.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;u&gt;MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;An associate degree (A. A.) or equivalent from two-year college or technical school; and 5 to 7+ years’ experience and/or training; or equivalent combination of education and experience. Minimum of 5 years working as an Electrical Designer I or II or at supervisors discretion.&lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;em&gt;We are an Equal Opportunity Employer and do not discriminate on the basis of race, color, religion, sex, national origin, age, disability, veteran status, genetic information, sexual orientation, gender identity, or any other legally protected status. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to any of these characteristics.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt; ]]>

<![CDATA[ &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Electrical Engineer III&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;Louisville, CO&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; &lt;strong&gt;100% on site role - in office presence required&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; Benefits: Access to Client Benefits Package&lt;br&gt; Pay Range: $115,000-$150,000&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;POSITION SUMMARY&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;Seeking an Electrical Engineer III to join our client’s team in the energy, mining, industrial power markets, and Integrated bio-energy solutions. The Electrical Engineer III will research, develop, design, and test electrical components, equipment and systems including power / control systems, applying principles and techniques of electrical engineering.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;RESPONSIBILITIES&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Design electrical equipment, facilities, components, products, and systems for industrial purposes. &lt;li&gt;Design and direct personnel in fabrication of control apparatus and equipment, and determine methods, procedures, and conditions for testing products such as generators, transformers, control devices, motors, conveyors, power distribution, and safety systems. &lt;li&gt;Develop applications of controls, instruments, and systems for industrial uses, including motors and conveyance systems; lead activities to ensure that manufacturing, construction, installation, and operation conform to functional specifications and customer requirements. &lt;li&gt;Direct and coordinate operation, maintenance and repair of equipment and systems in field installations utilizing computer-assisted engineering and design software and equipment to perform engineering tasks. &lt;li&gt;Perform specific and limited portions of a broader assignment of an experienced engineer. Lead a single group of Engineers, Designers and Technicians. &lt;li&gt;Independently evaluate, select, and apply standard practices and techniques in specific situations, adjust and correlate data, recognize discrepancies in the results, and follow operations through a series of related detailed steps or processes. &lt;li&gt;Ability to design a complete standard electrical engineering drawings package, which includes, power one-lines, control schematics, control panel layouts with bills of material, interconnection diagrams, cable schedules, cable tray design criteria, and cable tray drawings. &lt;li&gt;Ability to create program projects, modify, debug PLC software, and understand the various communication networks used. &lt;li&gt;Serve as the primary electrical resource for the installation and start-up of the assignment. &lt;li&gt;Ability to manage electrical contractors along with Modular Fabrication resources to complete unitized and pre-assembled work. &lt;li&gt;Collaborate with the estimation department to create and execute project estimations. &lt;li&gt;Work with project management to create schedules for assignments. Manage electrical portion of some projects. &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;REQUIREMENTS&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;Bachelor's degree in electrical engineering is required. &lt;li&gt;5-7+ years of experience in electrical engineering is required. &lt;li&gt;Power experience is a plus (i.e. power distribution centers, motor control centers, large frequency drives, medium voltage ) &lt;li&gt;Project management experience &lt;li&gt;AutoCAD and drafting experience beyond a basic level is preferred. &lt;li&gt;Experience developing drawings for fabrication of wire way systems are preferred. &lt;li&gt;Experience with selection and specification of switch gear, motor control centers, large generators, medium to high voltage transformers, water systems, support equipment and/or HVAC equipment is preferred. &lt;li&gt;Strong mechanical aptitude and hands-on experience are preferred. &lt;li&gt;Process knowledge of P&amp;ID’s. &lt;li&gt;Excellent communication skills are required. &lt;li&gt;EIT registration is preferred. &lt;li&gt;Microsoft Office proficiency &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;br&gt; &lt;em&gt;We are an Equal Opportunity Employer and do not discriminate on the basis of race, color, religion, sex, national origin, age, disability, veteran status, genetic information, sexual orientation, gender identity, or any other legally protected status.
